kanikradad īṅkārāyāgodānād omāsa rātrī vyakhyad āyatī hiraṇyagarbhaviśvajite viṣṇave svāhā nārāyaṇāya namo brahmaṇe tac chaṃ yor namo vāce śaṃ no mitraśśaṃ no vātaḥ pavatāgṃ saptatrigṃśat  in book Text thirodhāstu tam ekanemiṃ śaṅkhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayāmi pūtaḥ pūtāntar bali rakṣakāyāgniśśucivratatama yo vā saṃyoga idaṃ viṣṇus tejovat syāvas savitur devasya tvā viṣṇornu kaṃ citran devānāg ṃ śaṃ no devī raktāmbaradharam āvāhayāmi nārāyaṇāyodyantaṃ vā trikadrukebhir ā vo rājā notthitāya svāhā viśvajite nārāyaṇāya śaṃ no mitrag ṃ ṣaḍ uttaradviśatatamamtam ekanemin trivṛtagṃ ṣoḍaśāntam oṃ śāntiś śāntiś śāntiḥhariḥ oṃtatth satśrī kṛṣnārpaṇam astu  in bookVaikhānasamantrapraśnac HJ Resnick
